<script type="text/javascript">
	/** 定时 **/
	var countdownS = 300;
	var setShipErrTimeS = function(flagS, isProcess) {
		if (countdownS == 0 || isProcess == 1) {
			$("#expireVipClose").empty().text("关闭");
			$('#expireVipClose').removeAttr('disabled');
			countdownS = 300;
			flagS = 0;
		} else {
			$('#expireVipClose').attr("disabled", true);
			$("#expireVipClose").empty().text(countdownS+"s后可关闭");
			countdownS--;
		}
		if(flagS == 1){
			setTimeout("setShipErrTimeS("+ flagS +","+ isProcess +")",1000);
		}
	};
</script>

<script type="text/javascript">
    function timingDateEdit(){
        var newDateOjb = $dp.cal;
        var newY = newDateOjb.getP('y');
        var newM = newDateOjb.getP('M');
        var newD = newDateOjb.getP('d');
        var newH = newDateOjb.getP('H');
        var newm = newDateOjb.getP('m');
        var news = newDateOjb.getP('s');
        var newDate = newY + '-'+ newM + '-'+newD + ' '+newH + ':'+newm + ':'+news;
        newDate = Date.parse(new Date(newDate));
        var nowDate = Date.parse(new Date());
        if(/*nowDate > newDate || */(newDate - nowDate) < (1000*60) ){
            newDate += 1000*60*5;
        }
        newDate = new Date(newDate);
        newDate = newDate.format('yyyy-MM-dd hh:mm:ss');
        $dp.el.value = newDate;
    }
    $(document).on('change','#scheduleTimeType',function(){
        if($('#scheduleTimeType').val()==1){
            $('#scheduleTime0').css('display','none');
            $('#scheduleTime1').css('display','block');
        }else{
            $('#scheduleTime0').toggle();
            $('#scheduleTime1').toggle();
        }
    });

</script><!DOCTYPE HTML PUBLIC "-//W3C//DTD HTML 4.01 Transitional//EN"><script type="text/javascript" src="https://www.dianxiaomi.com/static/js/common/advancedTranslate.js?v=pi45.35"></script>

            dataType:'json',
            success:function (data) {
                if(!+data.code && data.result && data.result.result){
                    var result = data.result.result,
                        $smtProDiagnoseMsg = $('#smtProDiagnoseMsg'),
                        pLength = $smtProDiagnoseMsg.find('p').length + 1,
						domP = '';
                    if(result.requiredAttribute){
                        domP += '<p class="p5">'+ pLength +'、必填属性缺失</p>';
                        pLength++;
                    }
                    if(result.keyAttribute){
                        domP += '<p class="p5">'+ pLength +'、关键属性缺失</p>';
                        pLength++;
                    }
                    if(result.commonAttribute){
                        domP += '<p class="p5">'+ pLength +'、普通属性缺失</p>';
                        pLength++;
                    }
                    if(result.repeatSubject){
                        var subjectVal = $('#subject').val(),
                            repeatSubject = result.repeatSubject.split('$#$');
                        for(var i = 0;i < repeatSubject.length;i++){
                            if(repeatSubject[i]){
                                var reg = new RegExp(repeatSubject[i],'g');
                                subjectVal = subjectVal.replace(reg,'<span class="fRed fW600">'+repeatSubject[i]+'</span>');
                            }
                        }
                        domP += '<p class="p5">'+ pLength +'、标题包含重复单词：'+subjectVal+'</p>';
                        pLength++;
                    }
                    if(result.imageQuatity){
                        domP += '<p class="p5">'+ pLength +'、主图、属性图质量不佳：'+result.imageQuatity+' <a href="http://bbs.seller.aliexpress.com/bbs/read.php?tid=268404" target="_blank">点击此处</a> 查看速卖通各行业的图片要求，进行相应的修改！</p>';
                        pLength++;
                    }
                    if(result.detail){
                        domP += '<p class="p5">'+ pLength +'、PC端描述不含图片</p>';
                        pLength++;
                    }
                    if(result.mobileDetail){
                        domP += '<p class="p5">'+ pLength +'、移动端描述未开启</p>';
                        pLength++;
                    }
                    if(result.sale){
                        domP += '<p class="p5">'+ pLength +'、产品30天无销量</p>';
                        pLength++;
                    }
                    if(result.contrabndWord){
                        var contrabndWord = JSON.parse(result.contrabndWord),
                            values= '',
							msgStr = '',
                            detail = '',
                            subject = '',
                            mobileDetail = '';
                        for(var key in contrabndWord){
                            var contrabndWordVal = contrabndWord[key].split(',');
                            msgStr = '';
                            for(var i = 0;i < contrabndWordVal.length;i++){
                                if(contrabndWordVal[i]){
                                    msgStr += (!msgStr ? '' : '，') + '<span class="fRed fW600">'+contrabndWordVal[i]+'</span>';
                                }
                            }
                            if(key === 'detail'){
                                detail = '描述包含词：'+msgStr;
                            }else if(key === 'subject'){
                                subject = '标题包含词：'+msgStr;
                            }else if(key === 'mobileDetail'){
                                mobileDetail = '无线端描述包含词：'+msgStr;
                            }
                        }
                        values = subject ? subject + '。' : detail ? detail + '。' : mobileDetail ? mobileDetail + '。' : '';
                        domP += '<p class="p5">'+ pLength +'、标题、描述包含自定义检测词：'+values+'</p>';
                        pLength++;
                    }
                    if(result.stock){
                        domP += '<p class="p5">'+ pLength +'、库存数低于：'+data.stock+'</p>';
                        pLength++;
                    }
                    $smtProDiagnoseMsg.append(domP);
                    $('#smtProDiagnoseDiv').removeClass('myj-hide');

		if($("#productStateFail").val() == "publishFail" ) {
            var DeleteImageDetail = editorReplaceDisabledTag(editorReplaceAllBlank(smtStrHand.transitionHtml(getEditorData('myj-editor')))),
                ImageErrorNumber = 0,
                $parentDocument = $('<div></div>');

            $parentDocument.html(DeleteImageDetail);
            $.each($parentDocument.find('img'), function(i, j) {
                var $tempImg = new Image(),
                    $obj = $(j);

                $tempImg.src = j.src;
                $tempImg.onerror = function() {
                    $obj.remove();
                    ImageErrorNumber++;
                    $('.pictureErrorTip').addClass('block');
                    $('.pictureErrorTip span').html(ImageErrorNumber);
                }
            });

            // a标签的点击事件，清除失效图片
            $(document).off('click', '.pictureErrorTip .pictureErrorImgDeleteBox').on('click', '.pictureErrorTip .pictureErrorImgDeleteBox', function() {
                $('#confirmDelectImageModal').modal('show');

                DeleteImageDetail = editorReplaceDisabledTag(editorReplaceAllBlank(smtStrHand.transitionHtml(getEditorData('myj-editor'))));
                $parentDocument.html(DeleteImageDetail);
                var $img = $parentDocument.find('img'),
					imgLen = $img.length;

                ImageErrorNumber = 0;
                $.each($img, function(i, j) {
                    var $tempImg = new Image(),
                        $obj = $(j);

                    $tempImg.src = j.src;
                    $tempImg.onerror = function() {
                        $obj.remove();
                        ImageErrorNumber++;
                        if(ImageErrorNumber === imgLen){
                            setEditorData('myj-editor', $parentDocument.html());
                            $('.pictureErrorTip').removeClass('block');
                            $('#confirmDelectImageModal').modal('hide');
                        }
                    };
                    $tempImg.onload = function() {
                        ImageErrorNumber++;
                        if(ImageErrorNumber === imgLen){
                            setEditorData('myj-editor', $parentDocument.html());
                            $('.pictureErrorTip').removeClass('block');
                            $('#confirmDelectImageModal').modal('hide');
						}
                    };
                });
            });
		}

        (function() {
            var hm = document.createElement('script');
            hm.src = '//hm.baidu.com/hm.js?f8001a3f3d9bf5923f780580eb550c0b';
            var s = document.getElementsByTagName('script')[0];
            s.parentNode.insertBefore(hm, s);
        })();

        //图片缓存问题
		PRODUCT_ERROR_IMAGE.errImgListFn($('#myj-drop, #thumbnailsBox, #skuAttribute'), $('#productErrImgList')); //检查是否有图片地址不存在的图片

	/****************************图片upload****************************/
    $('#upload').click(function(){
        $('#uploadLocalIpt').val('').click();
    });
    //产品图片本地上传
    $(document).off('change', '#uploadLocalIpt').on('change', '#uploadLocalIpt', function(){
        var files = this.files,
            n,
            $canCloseLoading = $('#canCloseLoading');

        if(dxmState !== 'draft'){
            n = files.length + imgTotalNum;
            if(n > maxUploadNum){
                $canCloseLoading.modal('hide');
                $.fn.message({type:'error',msg:'最大支持'+maxUploadNum+'张图片,您还能选用'+(maxUploadNum - imgTotalNum)+'张!'});
                return;
            }
        }else{
            n = $('input[name="selectedImg"]:checked').length;
            if(n >= maxUploadNum){
                $canCloseLoading.modal('hide');
                $.fn.message({type: 'error', msg: '最大支持' + maxUploadNum + '张图片,您还能选用' + (maxUploadNum - n) + '张!'});
                return;
            }
        }

        $canCloseLoading.modal('show');
        wxPicUpload.newImgUploadFromLocal(files, {type: 'album', fullCid: '2195504-', isNeedTree: 0, upType: this.accept}, function(data, err){
            $canCloseLoading.modal('hide');
            if(err === 1){
                if(dxmState !== 'draft'){
                    // 生成展示图片
                    showImg('', getPicRealUrl(data.url));
                    $('#curImgNum').text(imgTotalNum);
                    checkNeedBitPicture();
                }else{
                    showImg('', getTinyPicRealUrl(data.url), 'myj-show', true);
                    OVERFLOW_IMG_HIDE.showMoreImgs();//只要上传新图片，隐藏的产品图片就要全部显示
                }
            }
        });
    });

    var SKU_IMG_ID = '',// 变种图片本地上传记录图片id
		STRAIGHT = '';
    var imageUpload = function(cid,straight){
        // 变种图片本地上传共用
        $('#skuImgUploadLocalIpt').val('').click();
        SKU_IMG_ID = cid;
        STRAIGHT = straight;
	};
    //图片接口改造，产品本地图片上传请求地址改新地址
    $('#skuImgUploadLocalIpt').off('change').on('change', function(){   //图片上传处理
        var files = this.files,
            skuImgId = SKU_IMG_ID;

        if(STRAIGHT !== 't') files = [files[0]];
        wxPicUpload.newImgUploadFromLocal(files, {type: 'album', fullCid: '2195504-', isNeedTree: 0, upType: this.accept}, function(data, err){
            if(err === 1){// 成功请求
                if(STRAIGHT === 't'){
                    if(getPicRealUrl(data.url)) {
                        var selImg = [];
                        selImg.push(getPicRealUrl(data.url));
                        batchMap.getPicProcess(selImg); //纯粹获取图片
                    }
                }else{
                    if($.trim(skuImgId)){ //sku图片上传
                        skuImg(skuImgId,getPicRealUrl(data.url));
                    }
                }
            }
        });
    });

    // 批量下载图片
    var batchDownloadImg = function() {
        var urls = '',
            fileName = '',
            uniqueKey = '';
        if($.trim(dxmState) === 'draft'){
            fileName = '速卖通_采集箱_编辑_';
            uniqueKey = "smtcaiji" + $("#productId").val();
            $("#img_show input[name='selectedImg']").each(function(){
                var urlDraft = $(this).closest('.out').find("img").attr("src");
                if(urlDraft){
                    if(urlDraft.indexOf("?") > 0 && urlDraft.indexOf("wxalbum-10001658") < 0){
                        urlDraft = urlDraft.substring(0, urlDraft.indexOf("?"));
                    }
                    urls += (!urls ? '' : ',') + urlDraft;
                }
            });
        }else{
            if($.trim(dxmState) === "online"){
                fileName = "速卖通_在线产品_编辑_";
                uniqueKey = "smtOnline" + $("#productId").val();
            }else if(!productStatusType){
                if($("#productId").val()){
                    fileName = "速卖通_待发布_编辑_";
                    uniqueKey = "smtWaitPublish" + $("#productId").val();
                }else{
                    fileName = "速卖通_创建产品_";
                    uniqueKey = 'smtCreateProduct' + '';
                }
            }
            $("#img_show img[data-names='auxiliaryImg']").each(function(){
                var rel = $(this).attr("src");
                if(rel){
                    if(rel.indexOf("?") > 0 && rel.indexOf("wxalbum-10001658") < 0){
                        rel = rel.substring(0, rel.indexOf("?"));
                    }
                    urls += (!urls ? '' : ',') + rel;
                }
            });
        }
        //取变种图片
        $(".myj-table .imgTd img").each(function(){
            var v = $.trim($(this).attr("src"));
            if(v && v !== "static/img/addImg.jpg"){
                if(v.indexOf("?") > 0 && v.indexOf("wxalbum-10001658") < 0){
                    v = v.substring(0, v.indexOf("?"));
                }
                urls += (!urls ? '' : ',') + v;
            }
        });
        if(!urls){
			$.fn.message({type: 'error', msg: '请至少选择一张图片'});
			return;
        }
        var data = {
            urls : urls,
            fileName : fileName,
            uniqueKey : uniqueKey
        };
        $("#batchCheckReplicaProgressBar").css("width", "0%");
        $("#batchCheckReplicaProcessNum").text("0");
        $("#reportShow").removeClass("fRed").html("正在导出中，请稍后...");
        $('#batchDownloadImageModal').modal('show');
        $('div[uid="downloadFill"]').removeClass('dropdown').find('button[uid="dropdown"]').removeClass('btn-primary').addClass('btn-default').attr('disabled',true).css('color','#000000');
        $.ajax({
            type:'POST',
            url: gitWinLocHref() + 'album/batchDownloadFromProduct.json',
            data:data,
            dataType:'json',
            success:function(back){
                var total = back.totalNum;
                var uuid = back.uuid;
                var p = 0;    // 记录进度条的值
                checkProcessStatus(uuid, function(data){
                    var num = Math.round(data.num / data.totalNum * 100),
                        status = "检测中...";
                    if(num < p && +data.code !== 1){
                        // 为了去掉变为n->0时的动画效果，在此先隐藏，然后再置0，最后再定时显示出来
                        $("#batchCheckReplicaProgressBar").css("display", "none");
                        setTimeout(function(){
                            $("#batchCheckReplicaProgressBar").css("display", "");
                        },1000);
                    }
                    p = num;
                    if(!+data.code){
                        $("#batchCheckReplicaProgressBar").css("width", num + "%");
                        $("#batchCheckReplicaProcessNum").text(data.num);
                        $("#reportShow").text("正在导出中，请稍后...");
                    }else if(+data.code === -1){
                        $("#batchCheckReplicaProgressBar").css("width", num + "%").removeClass("active");
                        $("#batchCheckReplicaProcessNum").text(data.num);
                        $("#reportShow").addClass("fRed").html(data.msg);
                    }else{
                        $("#batchCheckReplicaProgressBar").css("width", "100%").removeClass("active");
                        $("#batchCheckReplicaProcessNum").text(data.num);
                        $("#reportShow").html('导出文件已生成，文件将会在5分钟后失效,请立即下载<br/>');
                        $('div[uid="downloadFill"]').addClass('dropdown').find('button[uid="dropdown"]').removeClass('btn-default').addClass('btn-primary').attr('disabled',false).css('color','#FFFFFF');
                        $('.highSpeedDownload').find('a').attr('href',data.msg);
                        var msg = data.msg,
                            msgOver = getDownloadUrl(msg);
                        $('.standbDownload').find('a').attr('href',msgOver);
                    }
                });
            }
        });
    };
    $(document).on('click','span[removeTrMark="removeTrMark"]',function(){
        $(this).parent().parent().remove();
        $("#sourceTab tr[sourceUrlMarkTr='sourceUrlMarkTr']").each(function(i){
            $(this).find("span").first().text(i+1);
        });
        showAdd(2);
    });

	var jumpFindGoods = function(obj){
		var url = $.trim($(obj).parent().prev().val()),
			productUrl=null;
		if(url){
			url = encodeURIComponent(url);
			if(url.indexOf("1688.com") > 0) {
				productUrl = "https://www.dianxiaomi.com/alibabaSimilarSource/getSimilarUrl.htm?productUrl=" + url + "&pid=mm_3245507754_17966_17982&type=dijiakaifa&module=crawl"
				window.open(productUrl);
			}else if(url.indexOf("haiyingshuju.com/wish/") > 0){
				url="https://www.wish.com/c/"+url.toString().substring(url.indexOf("?pid=")+5);
				productUrl = "https://www.dianxiaomi.com/alibabaSimilarSource/getSimilarUrl.htm?productUrl="+url+"&pid=mm_3245507754_18189_18170&type=tongkuan&module=crawl"
				window.open(productUrl);
			}else {
				productUrl = "https://www.dianxiaomi.com/alibabaSimilarSource/getSimilarUrl.htm?productUrl="+url+"&pid=mm_3245507754_18189_18170&type=tongkuan&module=crawl"
				window.open(productUrl);
			}
		}else{
			if(false){
				if(false){
					var subject =$("#subject").val();
					url = "http://www.aliexpress.com/item/"+subject+"/.html";
					productUrl = "https://www.dianxiaomi.com/alibabaSimilarSource/getSimilarUrl.htm?productUrl="+url+"&pid=mm_3245507754_18189_18170&type=tongkuan&module=crawl"
					window.open(productUrl);
				}else{
					var imgUrl = $("#myj-drop li:first img").attr("src");
					window.open('https://www.dianxiaomi.com/alibabaSimilarSource/getSimilarUrl.htm?imgUrl=' + imgUrl + '&pid=mm_3245507754_17966_17982&type=tongkuan&module=product');
				}
			}else {
				var imgUrl = $("#myj-drop li:first img").attr("src");
				window.open('https://www.dianxiaomi.com/alibabaSimilarSource/getSimilarUrl.htm?imgUrl=' + imgUrl + '&pid=mm_3245507754_17966_17982&type=tongkuan&module=product');
			}
		}
	}

    //移除营销图片
    var thumbnailImgRe = function(obj){
        var imgUrl,
            className = $(obj).attr('data-flag');

        className === 'whiteFundusImg' ? imgUrl = 'https://www.dianxiaomi.com/static/img/addImg.jpg' : imgUrl = 'https://www.dianxiaomi.com/static/img/addImgThreeToFour.jpg?v=1';
		$(obj).closest('.thumbnailsSingle').find('.' + className).attr('src', imgUrl).end().find('.imgDivDown').addClass('no-click').end().find('.imgSize').addClass('hide').text('');
		$(obj).closest('.thumbnailsSingle').find('div[data-toggle="popover"]').popover('destroy').find('span.glyphicon').remove();
    };
